<time>1432702162990< /time><Rate>5< /Rate><Text>Ever since my permanent teeth started growing in, I've felt self-conscious about my smile. My friends and family tried to assure me that there was nothing wrong with my teeth, and my own dentist told me, "If you were my daughter, I'd tell you to learn to love your teeth," when I suggested getting cosmetic corrections. When I had a consultation with Dr. Nisson, he told me not only the exact improvements he could make to my smile, but the explanations as to why my teeth had twisted and shifted over the years into what I had come to accept in the mirror. It was because of Dr. Nisson's honesty, direct approach, and warm bedside manor that I decided to get braces.

This was a big decision for me, because I was not a teenager being brought into an orthodontist's office by my well-meaning parents. I was now a young adult, having hated my smile for ten years, and I decided to give myself braces as a birthday present in hopes that I'd like what I saw in the mirror for once. From the beginning, Dr. Nisson was clear and patient with me as I asked innumerable questions and 'what if's' about the before, during, and after process of wearing braces. He always gave me his full attention, and his staff were prompt and thorough with responding to my many phonecalls throughout the year.

Personally, I did not find wearing braces a hardship, or even very painful. When they came off, on May 28th, 2013, I became a new person. I didn't just have a beautiful new smile. I had confidence and pride.

In almost two years of enjoying my beautiful new smile, I have had no problems or reversals. I have returned several times to Dr. Nisson's office, but only to order and pick up additional retainers, and of course for hugs and smiles--I never resist a chance to show off my pearly whites! During every return visit, everyone in the office has been glad to see me, and Dr. Nisson still gives me his full attention for any little 'what if' question I may have. I can't recommend Dr. Nisson highly enough, and I thoroughly encourage anyone who has yearned for self-esteem reflected in their smile to make an appointment for a consultation. Yeah, this place rocks. Obviously you aren't here for the atmosphere, you're here for the burger, and this one is superior. Excellent toasted bun, fresh toppings, good, flavorful beef. The fries were crispy and the portions substantial. Seems like the garlic on them was slightly sauteed, instead of the usual raw garlic bite.
Wish I could have tried the milkshakes, but I was stuffed with the burger and fries. Glad I didn't get an extra pattie, despite the quality.

The restaurant is kind of hard to spot in the dark, unless you know what you are looking for.</review>

<date>1554519159207< /date><rating>3< /rating><Review>For about $8 you can get a single cheeseburger, fries, and a drink. A drive thru quarter pounder meal costs more than that. Despite constant mixups with orders delivered to the wrong table, the food arrived quickly. I would have to guess J's Burgers is trying to emulate the Double-Double folks with the style and ingredients on the burgers. Includes shredded lettuce, tomato, and onion. The difference is J's uses their own sauce, which is tasty, but a bit watery. (makes a mess by the time you get to the end of the burger). The fries are shoe string thin, way too greasy, and don't taste very good, just like the other guys. Limited soda fountain drinks.
They also offer kids meals, chicken sandwiches, onion rings, and milkshakes.
Convenient location on Spring Street with a tiny parking lot shared with the shoe store everyone loves to hate.
Open late-ish compared to other locally owned places.< /Review>< Pics>

I couldn't ask for a better cheeseburger, it really is very close to perfect. The fries are a single fry style similar to Inn and Out fries, good but not my favorite as they are overly oily. I didn't like the onion rings very much, they tasted a little under done. In my opinion they need to work on the decor inside, its very basic and creates an unpleasant mood if you're eating in. Overall its a great small town burger joint and I'll certainly return although I will phone my order in for pick up.</review>

Great burgers. Nice staff. This isn't a fast food burger, it alwayse seems to have that nice, fresh, "home-made" flavor. I dont go to many burger places because they are usually bland and disappointing. But ill never turn down a J's burger.  P.S.  theyr burgers with bacon added takes their great burgers to a whole new level.
